[30;1m1 | [0m[35m# Migrating Python Projects that used Data Files[0m
[30;1m2 | [0m[35m[0m
[30;1m3 | [0m[35mFor existing projects that used `setuptools` and optionally the[0m
[30;1m4 | [0m[35m`get_data_files()` function from `jupyter_packaging`, we offer a migration[0m
[30;1m5 | [0m[35mscript that will convert your project to use `hatchling`.[0m
[30;1m6 | [0m[35mThese projects can include Jupyter Kernels or Jupyter Server Extensions[0m
[30;1m7 | [0m[35mthat ship with `data_files`.[0m
[30;1m8 | [0m[35m[0m
